(cid:68)(cid:79)(cid:3)(cid:85)(cid:72)(cid:74)(cid:76)(cid:82)(cid:81)(cid:86)(cid:3)(cid:11)(cid:72)(cid:17)(cid:74)(cid:17)(cid:15)(cid:3)(cid:38)(cid:85)(cid:82)(cid:82)(cid:78)(cid:3)(cid:68)(cid:81)(cid:71)(cid:3)(cid:43)(cid:88)(cid:74)(cid:75)(cid:86)(cid:87)(cid:82)(cid:81)(cid:3)(cid:21)(cid:19)(cid:19)(cid:27)(cid:30)(cid:3)(cid:38)(cid:85)(cid:82)(cid:82)(cid:78)(cid:3) (cid:83)(cid:68)(cid:87)(cid:87)(cid:72)(cid:85)(cid:81)(cid:86)(cid:15)(cid:3)(cid:68)(cid:81)(cid:71)(cid:3)(cid:90)(cid:75)(cid:72)(cid:87)(cid:75)(cid:72)(cid:85)(cid:3)(cid:86)(cid:88)(cid:70)(cid:75)(cid:3)(cid:75)(cid:68)(cid:89)(cid:72)(cid:3)(cid:70)(cid:75)(cid:68)(cid:81)(cid:74)(cid:72)(cid:71)(cid:3)(cid:86)(cid:76)(cid:81)(cid:70)(cid:72)(cid:3)(cid:87)(cid:75)(cid:72)(cid:3) (cid:21)(cid:19)(cid:20)(cid:24)(cid:15)(cid:3)(cid:21)(cid:19)(cid:20)(cid:26)(cid:68)(cid:15)(cid:3)(cid:21)(cid:19)(cid:20)(cid:26)(cid:69)(cid:15)(cid:3)(cid:21)(cid:19)(cid:20)(cid:28)(cid:30)(cid:3)(cid:38)(cid:85)(cid:82)(cid:82)(cid:78)(cid:3)(cid:72)(cid:87)(cid:3)(cid:68)(cid:79)(cid:17)(cid:3)(cid:21)(cid:19)(cid:20)(cid:25)(cid:12)(cid:17)(cid:3)(cid:36)(cid:79)(cid:86)(cid:82)(cid:15)(cid:3) (cid:83)(cid:85)(cid:72)(cid:89)(cid:76)(cid:82)(cid:88)(cid:86)(cid:3)(cid:87)(cid:75)(cid:85)(cid:72)(cid:72)(cid:3)(cid:86)(cid:88)(cid:85)(cid:89)(cid:72)(cid:92)(cid:86)(cid:17) 1In the course of this study, Slade carefully vetted the record sheets for points reported in the prior surveys (Meltzer 1986a, b; Meltzer and Bever 1995; Bever and Meltzer 2007), and several anomalies were spotted. Some involved the removal of duplicate records, others the addition of specimens. Specifically, in the 1995 survey six points were recorded for Angelina County, four of these reported as coming from near the Angelina Rivefor (see Brown 1993, 1994). However, the specimens actually came from the bordering San Augustine County. The record has been corrected, which also explains the four extra points now in San Augustine County. A point recorded in the 1995 survey from Brazos County is actually from Waller County. The record sheet entry says that the point was recovered from a gravel bar from the river close to Interstate 10 near the Austin/Wharton County line. These coordinates place the point in Waller County, the first for that county, and not Bra- zos County. In Coke County one point was used twice, so was dropped, reducing the count from four to three in that county. Two duplicate records were found in Gaines County from the 1995 survey, and after dropping those two records, the Gaines County tally fell from 28 to 26. Also from 1995, a Harris County record was removed. Jefferson County was always going to prove difficult due to the circumstances and inconsistencies surrounding the recording of the points from the McFaddin Beach area. Surprisingly, Sladeâs review of the record sheets and paper archive that accompanied the survey proved less problematic than expected. After tallying up all the records that were compiled from the previous surveys that should be in the survey and removed the duplicate records, the count was off by just one specimen. The previous surveys calculated 97 (Bever and Meltzer 2007: Table 1), the revised total is 98, and with a further eight added from post-2007 records, the total now is 106. There were a few other duplicate records, but one last revised record deserves mention. The Kincaid Shelter site in Uvalde County (Collins et al. 1989) had a point missing from the survey that has now been included.
